## <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> endstone [#endstone]

**Modules:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`actor`](#endstone.actor) |
[`ban`](#endstone.ban) |
[`block`](#endstone.block) |
[`boss`](#endstone.boss) |
[`command`](#endstone.command) |
[`damage`](#endstone.damage) |
[`enchantments`](#endstone.enchantments) |
[`event`](#endstone.event) |
[`form`](#endstone.form) |
[`inventory`](#endstone.inventory) |
[`lang`](#endstone.lang) |
[`level`](#endstone.level) |
[`map`](#endstone.map) |
[`permissions`](#endstone.permissions) |
[`plugin`](#endstone.plugin) |
[`scheduler`](#endstone.scheduler) |
[`scoreboard`](#endstone.scoreboard) |
[`util`](#endstone.util) |

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`ColorFormat`](#endstone.ColorFormat) | All supported color and format codes.
[`EnchantmentRegistry`](#endstone.EnchantmentRegistry) |
[`GameMode`](#endstone.GameMode) | Represents the various type of game modes that Players may have.
[`ItemRegistry`](#endstone.ItemRegistry) |
[`Logger`](#endstone.Logger) | Logger class which can format and output varies levels of logs.
[`NamespacedKey`](#endstone.NamespacedKey) | Represents a string-based key which consists of two components - a namespace and a key.
[`OfflinePlayer`](#endstone.OfflinePlayer) | Represents a reference to a player identity and the data belonging to a player that is stored on the disk and can, thus, be retrieved without the player needing to be online.
[`Player`](#endstone.Player) | Represents a player.
[`Server`](#endstone.Server) | Represents a server implementation.
[`Skin`](#endstone.Skin) | Represents a player skin.

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-class"/> Server [#endstone.Server]

<div className="pl-[2em] mt-[1.25em]">

Represents a server implementation.

**Methods:**

<table>
<thead>
   <tr>
      <th>Name</th>
      <th>Description</th>
   </tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
    <tr key="broadcast">
        <td>[`broadcast`](#endstone.Server.broadcast)</td>
        <td>Broadcasts the specified message to every user with the given permission name.</td>
    </tr>
    <tr key="broadcast_message">
        <td>[`broadcast_message`](#endstone.Server.broadcast_message)</td>

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> actor [#endstone.actor]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`Actor`](#endstone.actor.Actor) | Represents a base actor in the level.
[`Item`](#endstone.actor.Item) | Represents a base actor in the level.
[`Mob`](#endstone.actor.Mob) | Represents a mobile entity (i.e. living entity), such as a monster or player.

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> command [#endstone.command]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`BlockCommandSender`](#endstone.command.BlockCommandSender) | Represents a block command sender.
[`Command`](#endstone.command.Command) | Represents a Command, which executes various tasks upon user input
[`CommandExecutor`](#endstone.command.CommandExecutor) | Represents a class which contains a single method for executing commands
[`CommandSender`](#endstone.command.CommandSender) | Represents a command sender.
[`CommandSenderWrapper`](#endstone.command.CommandSenderWrapper) | Represents a wrapper that forwards commands to the wrapped CommandSender and captures its output
[`ConsoleCommandSender`](#endstone.command.ConsoleCommandSender) | Represents a console command sender.

#### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-class"/> BlockCommandSender [#endstone.command.BlockCommandSender]

<div className="pl-[2em] mt-[1.25em]">

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> block [#endstone.command.BlockCommandSender.block]


### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> form [#endstone.form]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`ActionForm`](#endstone.form.ActionForm) | Represents a form with buttons that let the player take action.
[`Button`](#endstone.form.Button) | Represents a button with text and an optional icon.
[`Divider`](#endstone.form.Divider) | Represents a divider.
[`Dropdown`](#endstone.form.Dropdown) | Represents a dropdown with a set of predefined options.
[`Header`](#endstone.form.Header) | Represents a header with a label.
[`Label`](#endstone.form.Label) | Represents a text label.
[`MessageForm`](#endstone.form.MessageForm) | Represents a form with two buttons.
[`ModalForm`](#endstone.form.ModalForm) | Represents a modal form with controls.
[`Slider`](#endstone.form.Slider) | Represents a slider with a label.
[`StepSlider`](#endstone.form.StepSlider) | Represents a step slider with a set of predefined options.
[`TextInput`](#endstone.form.TextInput) | Represents a text input field.
[`Toggle`](#endstone.form.Toggle) | Represents a toggle button with a label.

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> inventory [#endstone.inventory]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`EquipmentSlot`](#endstone.inventory.EquipmentSlot) |
[`Inventory`](#endstone.inventory.Inventory) | Interface to the various inventories.
[`ItemFactory`](#endstone.inventory.ItemFactory) |
[`ItemMeta`](#endstone.inventory.ItemMeta) | Represents the metadata of a generic item.
[`ItemStack`](#endstone.inventory.ItemStack) | Represents a stack of items.
[`ItemType`](#endstone.inventory.ItemType) | Represents an item type.
[`MapMeta`](#endstone.inventory.MapMeta) | Represents the metadata for a map item.
[`PlayerInventory`](#endstone.inventory.PlayerInventory) | Interface to the inventory of a Player, including the four armor slots and any extra slots.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> add_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.add_item]

```python
add_item(*args) -> dict[int, ItemStack]
```

Stores the given ItemStacks in the inventory.
This will try to fill existing stacks and empty slots as well as it can.

The returned map contains what it couldn't store, where the key is the index, and the value is the ItemStack.
If all items are stored, it will return an empty dict.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> contents [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.contents]

```python
contents: list[ItemStack]
```

Returns all ItemStacks from the inventory

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> first_empty [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.first_empty]

```python
first_empty: int
```

Returns the first empty Slot.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> get_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.get_item]

```python
get_item(index:int) -> ItemStack
```

Returns the ItemStack found in the slot at the given index

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> is_empty [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.is_empty]

```python
is_empty: bool
```

Check whether this inventory is empty. An inventory is considered to be empty if there are no ItemStacks in any slot of this inventory.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> max_stack_size [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.max_stack_size]

```python
max_stack_size: int
```

Returns the maximum stack size for an ItemStack in this inventory.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> remove_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.remove_item]

```python
remove_item(*args) -> dict[int, ItemStack]
```

Removes the given ItemStacks from the inventory.
It will try to remove 'as much as possible' from the types and amounts you give as arguments.

The returned HashMap contains what it couldn't remove, where the key is the index, and the value is the ItemStack.
If all the given ItemStacks are removed, it will return an empty dict.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> set_item [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.set_item]

```python
set_item(index:int, item:ItemStack) -> None
```

Stores the ItemStack at the given index of the inventory.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> size [#endstone.inventory.Inventory.size]

```python
size: int
```

Returns the size of the inventory

</div>

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> map [#endstone.map]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`MapCanvas`](#endstone.map.MapCanvas) | Represents a canvas for drawing to a map. Each canvas is associated with a specific MapRenderer and represents that renderer's layer on the map.
[`MapRenderer`](#endstone.map.MapRenderer) | Represents a renderer for a map.
[`MapView`](#endstone.map.MapView) | Represents a map item.

```python
get_base_pixel_color(x:int, y:int) -> tuple[int, ...]
```

Get a pixel from the layers below this canvas.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> get_pixel_color [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.get_pixel_color]

```python
get_pixel_color(x:int, y:int) -> tuple[int, ...] | None
```

Get a pixel from the canvas.

If no color is set at the given position for this canvas, then None is returned and the color returned by get_base_pixel_color() is shown on the map

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-attribute"/> map_view [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.map_view]

```python
map_view: MapView
```

Get the map this canvas is attached to.

##### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-method"/> set_pixel_color [#endstone.map.MapCanvas.set_pixel_color]

```python
set_pixel_color(x:int, y:int, color:tuple[int, ...] | None) -> None
```

Draw a pixel to the canvas.

If None is used as color, then the color returned by get_base_pixel_color() is shown on the map.

</div>

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`Permissible`](#endstone.permissions.Permissible) | Represents an object that may become a server operator and can be assigned permissions.
[`Permission`](#endstone.permissions.Permission) | Represents a unique permission that may be attached to a Permissible
[`PermissionAttachment`](#endstone.permissions.PermissionAttachment) | Holds information about a permission attachment on a Permissible object
[`PermissionAttachmentInfo`](#endstone.permissions.PermissionAttachmentInfo) | Holds information on a permission and which PermissionAttachment provides it
[`PermissionDefault`](#endstone.permissions.PermissionDefault) | Represents the possible default values for permissions
[`PermissionLevel`](#endstone.permissions.PermissionLevel) |

### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-module"/> plugin [#endstone.plugin]

**Classes:**

Name | Description
---- | -----------
[`Plugin`](#endstone.plugin.Plugin) |
[`PluginCommand`](#endstone.plugin.PluginCommand) | Represents a Command belonging to a Plugin
[`PluginDescription`](#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription) | Represents the basic information about a plugin that the plugin loader needs to know.
[`PluginLoadOrder`](#endstone.plugin.PluginLoadOrder) | Represents the order in which a plugin should be initialized and enabled.
[`PluginLoader`](#endstone.plugin.PluginLoader) | Represents a plugin loader, which handles direct access to specific types of plugins
[`PluginManager`](#endstone.plugin.PluginManager) | Represents a plugin manager that handles all plugins from the Server
[`Service`](#endstone.plugin.Service) | Represents a list of methods.
[`ServiceManager`](#endstone.plugin.ServiceManager) | Represent a service manager that manages services and service providers.
[`ServicePriority`](#endstone.plugin.ServicePriority) | Represents various priorities of a provider.

#### <code className="doc-symbol doc-symbol-class"/> PluginDescription [#endstone.plugin.PluginDescription]

```python
PluginDescription(
    name: str,
    version: str,
    description: str | None = None,
    load: PluginLoadOrder | None = None,
    authors: list[str] | None = None,
    contributors: list[str] | None = None,
    website: str | None = None,
    prefix: str | None = None,
    provides: list[str] | None = None,
    depend: list[str] | None = None,
    soft_depend: list[str] | None = None,
    load_before: list[str] | None = None,
    default_permission: PermissionDefault | None = None,
    commands: list[Command] | None = None,
    permissions: list[Permission] | None = None,
    *args: list[Permission] | None,
    **kwargs: list[Permission] | None
)
```
